requests\\n   - Routes incoming HTTP requests to appropriate filter chains and ultimately to route selection\\n   - Integrates with the router filter (source/common/router/router.h/cc)\\n\\n2. **Core Route Matching Engine (source/common/router/config_impl.h/cc)**\\n   - RouteMatcher: The main route matching class that finds virtual hosts and routes for incoming requests\\n   - Implements findVirtualHost() to select the appropriate VirtualHostImpl based on request headers\\n   - Implements route() to get the final RouteEntry for a request\\n   - Supports wildcard virtual host matching with findWildcardVirtualHost() for both suffix and prefix matching\\n\\n3. **Virtual Host Selection (source/common/router/config_impl.h/cc)**\\n   - VirtualHostImpl: Encapsulates a collection of routes for a specific virtual host\\n   - Matches virtual hosts based on the :authority header and domain names\\n   - Handles SSL redirect requirements per virtual host\\n   - CommonVirtualHostImpl: Shared data for all routes within a virtual host, implementing the VirtualHost interface\\n   - Uses a MatchTree (source/common/matcher/matcher.h) for efficient route matching when enabled\\n\\n4. **Route Entry Implementation (source/common/router/config_impl.h/cc)**\\n   - RouteEntryImplBase: Base class for all route entry implementations\\n   - PathRouteEntryImpl: Matches routes based on path prefix\\n   - RegexRouteEntryImpl: Matches routes using regex patterns\\n   - UriTemplateMatcherRouteEntryImpl: Matches routes using URI templates\\n   - Each route entry encapsulates the action to take (cluster selection, redirect, direct response, etc.)\\n\\n5. **Route Action Dispatch (source/common/router/config_impl.h/cc)**\\n   - RouteMatchAction: Action used with the matching tree to specify which route to use\\n   - Routes are selected based on path matching, header matching, method matching, and other criteria\\n   - Header parsing (source/common/router/header_parser.h/cc) handles request/response header mutations\\n\\n6. **Advanced Matching Features**\\n   - MetadataMatchCriteria (source/common/router/metadatamatchcriteria_impl.h/cc): Matches routes based on metadata\\n   - TlsContextMatchCriteria (source/common/router/tls_context_match_criteria_impl.h/cc): Matches routes based on TLS context\\n   - Matcher framework (source/common/matcher/matcher.h): Generic matching tree implementation\\n   - HTTP matching inputs (source/common/http/matching/inputs.h/cc): Provides request data for matching evaluation\\n\\n7. **Scoped Routing (source/common/router/scoped_config_impl.h/cc)**\\n   - Supports scoped routes which allow different route configurations per scope (e.g., per request property)\\n   - RDS support (source/common/router/rds_impl.h/cc): Route Discovery Service for dynamic route configuration\\n\\n8. **Route Dispatch and Filtering (source/common/router/router.h/cc)**\\n   - Router::Filter: The HTTP stream decoder filter that uses route matching to forward requests\\n   - Applies matched route's actions (cluster selection, retries, rate limiting, etc.)\\n   - UpstreamRequest
